# Django ORM Raw SQL Injection Prevention

## Your Task

Find all Python source files in django/django that handle raw SQL queries and prevent SQL injection: the RawSQL expression sanitization, the raw() queryset method parameter binding, and the cursor.execute() parameterization enforcement.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the security domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/django--674eda1c.

    22→class SQLiteNumericMixin:

    24→    Some expressions with output_field=DecimalField() must be cast to

    28→    def as_sqlite(self, compiler, connection, **extra_context):

    32→                sql = "(CAST(%s AS NUMERIC))" % sql
    33→        except FieldError:
    34→            pass
    35→        return sql, params

  1263→                            parent_field.name, allow_joins, reuse, summarize
  1264→                        )

  1267→            query, allow_joins, reuse, summarize, for_save

150:class RawQuery:
39-assistanttool_useRead

   150→class RawQuery:
   151→    """A single raw SQL query."""
   152→
   153→    def __init__(self, sql, using, params=()):
   154→        self.params = params
   155→        self.sql = sql
   156→        self.using = using
   157→        self.cursor = None
   158→
   159→        # Mirror some properties of a normal query so that
   160→        # the compiler can be used to process results.
   161→        self.low_mark, self.high_mark = 0, None  # Used for offset/limit
   162→        self.extra_select = {}
   163→        self.annotation_select = {}
   164→
   165→    def chain(self, using):
   166→        return self.clone(using)
   167→
   168→    def clone(self, using):
   169→        return RawQuery(self.sql, using, params=self.params)
   170→
   171→    def get_columns(self):
   172→        if self.cursor is None:
   173→            self._execute_query()
   174→        converter = connections[self.using].introspection.identifier_converter
   175→        return [converter(column_meta[0]) for column_meta in self.cursor.description]
   176→
   177→    def __iter__(self):
   178→        # Always execute a new query for a new iterator.
   179→        # This could be optimized with a cache at the expense of RAM.
   180→        self._execute_query()
   181→        if not connections[self.using].features.can_use_chunked_reads:
   182→            # If the database can't use chunked reads we need to make sure we
   183→            # evaluate the entire query up front.
   184→            result = list(self.cursor)
   185→        else:
   186→            result = self.cursor
   187→        return iter(result)

100-usertool_resultRead
   150→class RawQuery:
   151→    """A single raw SQL query."""
   152→
   153→    def __init__(self, sql, using, params=()):
   154→        self.params = params
   155→        self.sql = sql
   156→        self.using = using
   157→        self.cursor = None
   158→
   159→        # Mirror some properties of a normal query so that
   160→        # the compiler can be used to process results.
   161→        self.low_mark, self.high_mark = 0, None  # Used for offset/limit
   162→        self.extra_select = {}
   163→        self.annotation_select = {}
   164→
   165→    def chain(self, using):
   166→        return self.clone(using)
   167→
   168→    def clone(self, using):
   169→        return RawQuery(self.sql, using, params=self.params)
   170→
   171→    def get_columns(self):
   172→        if self.cursor is None:
   173→            self._execute_query()
   174→        converter = connections[self.using].introspection.identifier_converter
   175→        return [converter(column_meta[0]) for column_meta in self.cursor.description]
   176→
   177→    def __iter__(self):
   178→        # Always execute a new query for a new iterator.
   179→        # This could be optimized with a cache at the expense of RAM.
   180→        self._execute_query()
   181→        if not connections[self.using].features.can_use_chunked_reads:
   182→            # If the database can't use chunked reads we need to make sure we
   183→            # evaluate the entire query up front.
   184→            result = list(self.cursor)
   185→        else:
   186→            result = self.cursor

   550→    def adapt_unknown_value(self, value):
   551→        """
   552→        Transform a value to something compatible with the backend driver.
   553→
   554→        This method only depends on the type of the value. It's designed for
   555→        cases where the target type isn't known, such as .raw() SQL queries.
   556→        As a consequence it may not work perfectly in all circumstances.
   557→        """
   558→        if isinstance(value, datetime.datetime):  # must be before date
   559→            return self.adapt_datetimefield_value(value)
   560→        elif isinstance(value, datetime.date):
   561→            return self.adapt_datefield_value(value)
   562→        elif isinstance(value, datetime.time):
   563→            return self.adapt_timefield_value(value)
   564→        elif isinstance(value, decimal.Decimal):
   565→            return self.adapt_decimalfield_value(value)
   566→        else:
   567→            return value

  1050→class Func(SQLiteNumericMixin, Expression):
  1051→    """An SQL function call."""
  1052→
  1053→    function = None
  1054→    template = "%(function)s(%(expressions)s)"
  1055→    arg_joiner = ", "
  1056→    arity = None  # The number of arguments the function accepts.
  1057→
  1058→    def __init__(self, *expressions, output_field=None, **extra):
  1059→        if self.arity is not None and len(expressions) != self.arity:
  1060→            raise TypeError(
  1061→                "'%s' takes exactly %s %s (%s given)"
  1062→                % (
  1063→                    self.__class__.__name__,
  1064→                    self.arity,
  1065→                    "argument" if self.arity == 1 else "arguments",
  1066→                    len(expressions),
  1067→                )
  1068→            )
  1069→        super().__init__(output_field=output_field)
  1070→        self.source_expressions = self._parse_expressions(*expressions)
  1071→        self.extra = extra
  1072→
  1073→    def __repr__(self):
  1074→        args = self.arg_joiner.join(str(arg) for arg in self.source_expressions)
  1075→        extra = {**self.extra, **self._get_repr_options()}
  1076→        if extra:
  1077→            extra = ", ".join(
  1078→                str(key) + "=" + str(val) for key, val in sorted(extra.items())
  1079→            )
  1080→            return "{}({}, {})".format(self.__class__.__name__, args, extra)
  1081→        return "{}({})".format(self.__class__.__name__, args)
  1082→

  1085→        return {}

   284→    def last_executed_query(self, cursor, sql, params):
   285→        """
   286→        Return a string of the query last executed by the given cursor, with
   287→        placeholders replaced with actual values.
   288→
   289→        `sql` is the raw query containing placeholders and `params` is the
   290→        sequence of parameters. These are used by default, but this method
   291→        exists for database backends to provide a better implementation
   292→        according to their own quoting schemes.
   293→        """
   294→
   295→        # Convert params to contain string values.
   296→        def to_string(s):
   297→            return force_str(s, strings_only=True, errors="replace")
   298→
   299→        if isinstance(params, (list, tuple)):
   300→            u_params = tuple(to_string(val) for val in params)
   301→        elif params is None:
   302→            u_params = ()
   303→        else:
   304→            u_params = {to_string(k): to_string(v) for k, v in params.items()}
   305→
   306→        return "QUERY = %r - PARAMS = %r" % (sql, u_params)
   307→

## Summary

The analysis found **12 key Python files** implementing SQL injection prevention across three main mechanisms:

### 1. **RawSQL Expression Sanitization**
- `django/db/models/expressions.py` - RawSQL class that separates SQL from parameters

### 2. **raw() QuerySet Method Parameter Binding**
- `django/db/models/query.py` - QuerySet.raw() method and RawQuerySet class
- `django/db/models/sql/query.py` - RawQuery class with critical _execute_query() method that adapts parameters to database types

### 3. **cursor.execute() Parameterization Enforcement**
- `django/db/backends/utils.py` - CursorWrapper that ensures all database access uses parameterized queries
- `django/db/backends/base/operations.py` - adapt_unknown_value() and quote_name() methods for parameter adaptation and identifier escaping
- Database-specific operations files for PostgreSQL, MySQL, SQLite, and Oracle

### Key SQL Injection Prevention Mechanisms:
1. **Parameterized Execution**: SQL and parameters kept separate throughout
2. **Parameter Adaptation**: Type conversion prevents type-based injection
3. **Identifier Quoting**: Table/column names properly escaped
4. **CursorWrapper Abstraction**: Centralized enforcement across all backends
5. **Expression-Based Building**: All queries built through expression objects maintaining separation
